             <div class="dslc-modules-area dslc-col dslc-12-col dslc-last-col" data-size="12">
              <div class="dslc-module-front dslc-module-DSLC_Separator dslc-in-viewport-check dslc-in-viewport-anim-none dslc-module-handle-like-regular" data-dslc-anim="none" data-dslc-anim-delay="0" data-dslc-anim-easing="ease" data-dslc-module-id="DSLC_Separator" data-dslc-module-size="12" data-module-id="5346" id="dslc-module-5346">

             <div class="dslc-modules-area dslc-col dslc-8-col dslc-first-col" data-size="8">
              <div class="dslc-module-front dslc-module-DSLC_TP_Content dslc-in-viewport-check dslc-in-viewport-anim-none dslc-module-handle-like-regular" data-dslc-anim="none" data-dslc-anim-delay="0" data-dslc-anim-easing="ease" data-dslc-module-id="DSLC_TP_Content" data-dslc-module-size="12" data-module-id="5347" id="dslc-module-5347">
               <div class="dslc-tp-content">
                <div class="ftpimagefix" style="float: left;">
                 <a href="http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/blogspot/ATHs/~3/eWRtuu6vwL0/fighting-bad-advertising-practices-on.html" target="_blank">
                  <img alt="" border="0" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-g3VmanCPYTE/VM_sDgmXcnI/AAAAAAAABQs/FJ2vfS-kPg8/s1600/Google_BadAds_Infographic_Feb02-Final.jpg" width="500"/>
                 </a>
                </div>
                <div dir="ltr">
                 Online advertising helps fund content and businesses on the web, from small family-owned shops to large publishers. While online advertising helps the web to work for all of us, this ecosystem can also attract bad actors that aim to misuse ads for harmful or deceptive purposes.We work hard to keep our advertising ecosystem clean for users, advertisers, and publishers, and continue to invest substantial resources to stop
                </div>
                <p>
                 This is a constantly evolving fight. Bad actors continually create more sophisticated systems and scams, so we too are continually evolving our practices, technology, and methodology in fighting these bad ads. The security of our users is the foundation of our ecosystem, and well continue to work tirelessly to keep people safe online. If youd like to provide feedback on specific ads or our policies, check out our
                 <a href="https://support.google.com/adwords/troubleshooter/4578507?rd=1" target="_blank">
                  online form
                 </a>
                 .
                </p>
                <p>
                 <i>
                  Posted by Vikaram Gupta, Director, Ads Engineering
                 </i>
                </p>
